\hypertarget{classamici_1_1_model}{}\doxysubsection{Model Class Reference}
\label{classamici_1_1_model}\index{Model@{Model}}


The \mbox{\hyperlink{classamici_1_1_model}{Model}} class represents an A\+M\+I\+CI O\+D\+E/\+D\+AE model. The model can compute various model related quantities based on symbolically generated code.  




{\ttfamily \#include $<$model.\+h$>$}
